\doxysection{physac.\+h}
\hypertarget{lib_2_raylib_erosion_standalone-main_2raylib_2src_2physac_8h_source}{}\label{lib_2_raylib_erosion_standalone-main_2raylib_2src_2physac_8h_source}\index{C:/Users/HP/Documents/GitHub/Minero-\/Game/lib/RaylibErosionStandalone-\/main/raylib/src/physac.h@{C:/Users/HP/Documents/GitHub/Minero-\/Game/lib/RaylibErosionStandalone-\/main/raylib/src/physac.h}}
\mbox{\hyperlink{lib_2_raylib_erosion_standalone-main_2raylib_2src_2physac_8h}{Go to the documentation of this file.}}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ Physac\ v1.0\ -\/\ 2D\ Physics\ library\ for\ videogames}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ Physac\ is\ a\ small\ 2D\ physics\ engine\ written\ in\ pure\ C.\ The\ engine\ uses\ a\ fixed\ time-\/step\ thread\ loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ to\ simluate\ physics.\ A\ physics\ step\ contains\ the\ following\ phases:\ get\ collision\ information,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ apply\ dynamics,\ collision\ solving\ and\ position\ correction.\ It\ uses\ a\ very\ simple\ struct\ for\ physic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ bodies\ with\ a\ position\ vector\ to\ be\ used\ in\ any\ 3D\ rendering\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_STATIC\ (defined\ by\ default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ generated\ implementation\ will\ stay\ private\ inside\ implementation\ file\ and\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ internal\ symbols\ and\ functions\ will\ only\ be\ visible\ inside\ that\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_NO\_THREADS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ generated\ implementation\ won't\ include\ pthread\ library\ and\ user\ must\ create\ a\ secondary\ thread\ to\ call\ PhysicsThread().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ It\ is\ so\ important\ that\ the\ thread\ where\ PhysicsThread()\ is\ called\ must\ not\ have\ v-\/sync\ or\ any\ other\ CPU\ limitation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Avoid\ raylib.h\ header\ inclusion\ in\ this\ file.\ Data\ types\ defined\ on\ raylib\ are\ defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ internally\ in\ the\ library\ and\ input\ management\ and\ drawing\ functions\ must\ be\ provided\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ user\ (check\ library\ implementation\ for\ further\ details).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_DEBUG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Traces\ log\ messages\ when\ creating\ and\ destroying\ physics\ bodies\ and\ detects\ errors\ in\ physics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ calculations\ and\ reference\ exceptions;\ it\ is\ useful\ for\ debug\ purposes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_MALLOC()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ PHYSAC\_FREE()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ You\ can\ define\ your\ own\ malloc/free\ implementation\ replacing\ stdlib.h\ malloc()/free()\ functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Otherwise\ it\ will\ include\ stdlib.h\ and\ use\ the\ C\ standard\ library\ malloc()/free()\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ NOTE\ 1:\ Physac\ requires\ multi-\/threading,\ when\ InitPhysics()\ a\ second\ thread\ is\ created\ to\ manage\ physics\ calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ NOTE\ 2:\ Physac\ requires\ static\ C\ library\ linkage\ to\ avoid\ dependency\ on\ MinGW\ DLL\ (-\/static\ -\/lpthread)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ Use\ the\ following\ code\ to\ compile:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ gcc\ -\/o\ \$(NAME\_PART).exe\ \$(FILE\_NAME)\ -\/s\ -\/static\ -\/lraylib\ -\/lpthread\ -\/lopengl32\ -\/lgdi32\ -\/lwinmm\ -\/std=c99}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
